It delivered and assembled the fourth starboard\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/S6_truss" title="S6 truss">\n        Integrated Truss Segment (S6)\n       </a>\n       , and the fourth set of solar arrays and batteries to the station. The launch took place on 15 March 2009, at 19:43 EDT.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nyt2_3-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-nyt2-3">\n         [3]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n  <a href="#cite_note-march4-5">\n         [5]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <i>\n        Discovery\n       </i>\n       successfully landed on 28 March 2009, at 15:13\xc2\xa0pm EDT.\n This crew would have consisted of:\n      </p>\n      <table class="wikitable plainrowheaders">\n       <tr>\n        <th style="width:150px;">\n         <a href="/wiki/Astronaut_ranks_and_positions" title="Astronaut ranks and positions">\n          Position\n         </a>\n        </th>\n        <th scope="col" style="width:150px;">\n         Launching Astronaut\n        </th>\n        <th scope="col" style="width:150px;">\n         Landing Astronaut\n        </th>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Commander\n        </th>\n        <td colspan="2">\n         <a href="/wiki/Steven_Lindsey" title="Steven Lindsey">\n          Steven W. Expedition 8\n         </a>\n         <br/>\n         ISS Flight Engineer\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Mission_payload">\n        Mission payload\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-119&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Mission payload">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <p>\n       STS-119 delivered the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/ISS_Solar_Arrays" title="ISS Solar Arrays">\n        S6 solar arrays\n       </a>\n       to the\n       <a href="/wiki/International_Space_Station" title="International Space Station">\n        space station\n       </a>\n       , completing the construction of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Integrated_Truss_Structure" title="Integrated Truss Structure">\n        Integrated Truss Structure\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-8">\n        <a href="#cite_note-8">\n         [8]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       STS-119 also carried several experiments, including the Shuttle Ionospheric Modification with Pulsed Local EXhaust (SIMPLEX), Shuttle Exhaust Ion Turbulence Experiments (SEITE), and Maui Analysis of Upper Atmospheric Injections (MAUI). STS-119 was also used for the "Boundary Layer Transition Detailed Test Objective" experiment. One tile of the thermal protection system was raised 0.25 inches (6.4\xc2\xa0mm) above the others so that, at about\n       <a href="/wiki/Mach_number" title="Mach number">\n        Mach\n       </a>\n       15 during reentry, a\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Boundary_layer_transition" title="Boundary layer transition">\n        boundary layer transition\n       </a>\n       would be initiated.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-9">\n        <a href="#cite_note-9">\n         [9]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       This experiment was repeated during\n       <a href="/wiki/STS-128" title="STS-128">\n        STS-128\n       </a>\n       with the tile raised to 0.35 inches (8.9\xc2\xa0mm), tripping at Mach 18 to produce more heat.\n      </p>\n      <table class="wikitable">\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n         Location\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         Cargo\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         Mass\n        </th>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         Bays 1\xe2\x80\x932\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         Orbiter Docking System\n         <br/>\n         <a href="/wiki/Extravehicular_Mobility_Unit" title="Extravehicular Mobility Unit">\n          EMU\n         </a>\n         3017 / EMU 3006\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         1,800 kilograms (4,000\xc2\xa0lb)\n         <br/>\n         ~260 kilograms (570\xc2\xa0lb)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         Bay 3P\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         Shuttle Power\n         <br/>\n         Distribution Unit (SPDU)\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         ~17 kilograms (37\xc2\xa0lb)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         Bays 3\xe2\x80\x9313\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/ISS_Solar_Arrays" title="ISS Solar Arrays">\n          S6 Truss\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         14,088 kilograms (31,059\xc2\xa0lb)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         Starboard Sill\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/Orbiter_Boom_Sensor_System" title="Orbiter Boom Sensor System">\n          Orbiter Boom Sensor System\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         ~382 kilograms (842\xc2\xa0lb)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         Port Sill\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/Canadarm" title="Canadarm">\n          Canadarm\n         </a>\n         202\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         410 kilograms (900\xc2\xa0lb)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <b>\n          Total:\n         </b>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <b>\n          16,957 kilograms (37,384\xc2\xa0lb)\n         </b>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Mission_background">\n        Mission background\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-119&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit 156th NASA manned space flight\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        125th shuttle mission since\n        <a href="/wiki/STS-1" title="STS-1">\n         STS-1\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        36th Flight of\n        <i>\n         Discovery\n        </i>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        100th post-\n        <i>\n         <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Challenger" title="Space Shuttle </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Shuttle_processing">\n        Shuttle processing\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-119&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Shuttle processing">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Space_Shuttle_Discovery_under_a_full_moon,_03-11-09.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2339" data-file-width="1875" height="274" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/57/Space_Shuttle_Discovery_under_a_full_moon%2C_03-11-09.jpg/220px-Space_Shuttle_Discovery_under_a_full_moon%2C_03-11-09.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/57/Space_Shuttle_Discovery_under_a_full_moon%2C_03-11-09.jpg/330px-Space_Shuttle_Discovery_under_a_full_moon%2C_03-11-09.jpg 1.5x, </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Space_Shuttle_Discovery_under_a_full_moon,_03-11-09.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Space Shuttle\n         <i>\n          Discovery\n         </i>\n         on the morning of 11 March 2009.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       <span class="nowrap">\n        <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle" title="Space Shuttle">\n         Space Shuttle\n        </a>\n       </span>\n       <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Discovery" title="Space Shuttle Discovery">\n        <i>\n         Discovery\n        </i>\n       </a>\n       moved from its\n       <a href="/wiki/Orbiter_Processing_Facility" title="Orbiter Processing Facility">\n        Orbiter Processing Facility\n       </a>\n       to the\n       <a href="/wiki/Vehicle_Assembly_Building" title="Vehicle Assembly Building">\n        Vehicle Assembly Building\n       </a>\n       on 7 January 2009.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-wdbo_10-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-wdbo-10">\n         [10]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The payload of the S6 truss segment, solar arrays and batteries were delivered to\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Launch_Complex_39" title="Launch Complex 39">\n        Launch pad 39A\n       </a>\n       on 11 January.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ft2_11-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ft2-11">\n         [11]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <i>\n        Discovery\n       </i>\n       moved to the launch pad 39A on 14 January 2009. The move began at 05:17 EST, and was completed at 12:16 EST.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Pad2_12-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Pad2-12">\n         [12]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The STS-119 crew was at\n       <a href="/wiki/Kennedy_Space_Center" title="Kennedy Space Center">\n        Kennedy Space Center\n       </a>\n       from 19\xe2\x80\x9322 January 2009 for the\n       <a href="/wiki/Terminal_countdown_demonstration_test" title="Terminal countdown demonstration test">\n        Terminal Countdown Demonstration Test\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-tcdt_13-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-tcdt-13">\n         [13]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On 21\xe2\x80\x9322 January 2009, mission managers met for the program level Flight Readiness Review (FRR). Following the FRR, mission managers recommended evaluating the hydrogen flow control valves on\n       <i>\n        Discovery\n       </i>\n       , and set a new target launch date of 19 February 2009.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-feb19_14-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-feb19-14">\n         [14]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tleft">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Shuttle_gaseous_hydrogen_flow_control_valve.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2008" data-file-width="3000" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bb/Shuttle_gaseous_hydrogen_flow_control_valve.jpg/220px-Shuttle_gaseous_hydrogen_flow_control_valve.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bb/Shuttle_gaseous_hydrogen_flow_control_valve.jpg/330px-Shuttle_gaseous_hydrogen_flow_control_valve.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bb/Shuttle_gaseous_hydrogen_flow_control_valve.jpg/440px-Shuttle_gaseous_hydrogen_flow_control_valve.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Shuttle_gaseous_hydrogen_flow_control_valve.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         The type of valve that was an interim concern.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Due to the breakage of one of three flow\n       <a href="/wiki/Control_valve" title="Control valve">\n        control valves\n       </a>\n       on the previous flight,\n       <a href="/wiki/STS-126" title="STS-126">\n        STS-126\n       </a>\n       , the flow valves of all orbiters were subjected to tests to determine if\n       <i>\n        Discovery\n       </i>\n       was safe to fly.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-sfn21_15-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-sfn21-15">\n         [15]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       These valves are used to synchronize the flow of\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Gaseous_hydrogen" title="Gaseous hydrogen">\n        gaseous hydrogen\n       </a>\n       between the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_External_Tank" title="Space Shuttle External Tank">\n        external fuel tank\n       </a>\n       and the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Main_Engine" title="Space Shuttle Main Engine">\n        Space Shuttle Main Engines\n       </a>\n       , creating an even flow.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fvfs_16-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fvfs-16">\n         [16]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Following the testing of the valves, mission managers decided to postpone the launch, and engineers were asked to replace the suspect flow valves with valves that had less flight time.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-sfn24_17-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-sfn24-17">\n         [17]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Following the replacement of the valves, the Mission Management Team gave the approval for launch, and scheduled it for 11 March 2009.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-mar11_18-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-mar11-18">\n         [18]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The astronauts arrived at the Kennedy Space Center on 8 March 2009 to prepare for launch. The 11 March 2009 launch was scrubbed due to a leak in a liquid hydrogen vent line between the shuttle and the external tank.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-autogenerated1_19-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-autogenerated1-19">\n         [19]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On 15 March 2009, the shuttle successfully lifted off from pad 39A.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nyt2_3-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-nyt2-3">\n         [3]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fox1_20-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fox1-20">\n         [20]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The leak problem manifested itself again during\n       <a href="/wiki/STS-127" title="STS-127">\n        STS-127\n       </a>\n       which led to a thorough test. The root cause was found to be a misalignment in the GUCP (Ground Umbilical Carrier Plate) which was set right leading to a successful flight.\n      </p>\n      <table class="wikitable">\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n         Attempt\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         Planned\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         Result\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         Turnaround\n        </th>\n </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         1\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <span class="sortkey" style="display:none;">\n          2009-03-11 21:20:14 !\n         </span>\n         <span class="sorttext">\n          11 Mar 2009, 9:20:14 pm\n         </span>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         scrubbed\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         ---\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         technical\n        </td>\n        <td>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         leak in a liquid hydrogen vent line\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-mar11_18-1">\n          <a href="#cite_note-mar11-18">\n           [18]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         2\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <span class="sortkey" style="display:none;">\n          2009-03-15 19:43:44 !\n         </span>\n         <span class="sorttext">\n          15 Mar 2009, 7:43:44 pm\n         </span>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         successful\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         3 days, 22 hours, 23 minutes\n        </td>\n        <td>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Mission_timeline">\n        Mission timeline\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-119&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Mission timeline">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="15_March_(Flight_day_1,_Launch)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="15_March_.28Flight_day_1.2C_Launch.29">\n        15 March (Flight day 1, Launch)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-119&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: 15 March (Flight day 1, Launch)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-119_Discovery_liftoff.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3000" data-file-width="2357" height="280" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/45/STS-119_Discovery_liftoff.jpg/220px-STS-119_Discovery_liftoff.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/45/STS-119_Discovery_liftoff.jpg/330px-STS-119_Discovery_liftoff.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/45/STS-119_Discovery_liftoff.jpg/440px-STS-119_Discovery_liftoff.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:STS-119_Discovery_liftoff.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Discovery" title="Space Shuttle Discovery">\n          Space Shuttle\n          <i>\n           Discovery\n          </i>\n         </a>\n         lifts off from\n         <a href="/wiki/Kennedy_Space_Center" title="Kennedy Space Center">\n          Kennedy Space Center\n         </a>\n         .\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Space Shuttle\n       <i>\n        Discovery\n       </i>\n       launched on time at 19:43 EDT without any issues. Upon initial review of early ascent imagery, mission managers did not see anything out of the ordinary with debris at launch. "We didn\'t see anything at all in the first quick look," noted\n       <a href="/wiki/William_H._Gerstenmaier" title="William H. Gerstenmaier">\n        Bill Gerstenmaier\n       </a>\n       , Associate Administrator for Space Operations, during the post-launch news conference.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-cbs315_21-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-cbs315-21">\n         [21]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       "I\xe2\x80\x99ve seen a lot of launches," commented Launch Director\n       <a href="/wiki/Michael_D._Leinbach" title="Michael D. Leinbach">\n        Michael D. Leinbach\n       </a>\n       during the conference, "and this was the most visibly beautiful launch I\xe2\x80\x99ve ever seen."\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nyt2_3-3">\n        <a href="#cite_note-nyt2-3">\n         [3]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-cbs315_21-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-cbs315-21">\n         [21]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       After reaching orbit, the STS-119 crew got to work on their orbit operations, opening the payload bay doors, deploying the\n       <a href="/wiki/Ku_band" title="Ku band">\n        Ku band\n       </a>\n       antenna, and activating and checking out the shuttle\'s\n       <a href="/wiki/Canadarm" title="Canadarm">\n        robotic arm\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nyt2_3-4">\n        <a href="#cite_note-nyt2-3">\n         [3]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fox1_20-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fox1-20">\n         [20]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The crew also downlinked the imagery taken of the external tank separation.\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Bat_stowaway">\n        Bat stowaway\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-119&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Bat stowaway">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <div class="thumb tleft">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-119_bat.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="494" data-file-width="647" height="168" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f6/STS-119_bat.jpg/220px-STS-119_bat.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f6/STS-119_bat.jpg/330px-STS-119_bat.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f6/STS-119_bat.jpg/440px-STS-119_bat.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:STS-119_bat.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Bat clinging to the External Tank.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       During the countdown a\n       <a href="/wiki/Bat" title="Bat">\n        bat\n       </a>\n       was seen to be resting on the external tank.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-22">\n        <a href="#cite_note-22">\n         [22]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       What was originally believed to be a\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Fruit_bat" title="Fruit bat">\n        fruit bat\n       </a>\n       was revealed to have been a\n       <a href="/wiki/Free-tailed_bat" title="Free-tailed bat">\n        free-tailed bat\n       </a>\n       that clung onto the fuel tank during the launch. NASA observers had believed the bat would fly off once the shuttle started to launch, but it did not, and it was probably shaken off and incinerated by the rocket exhaust. A bat doctor, analyzing pictures, believed the bat had a broken wing which made it unable to fly off.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-23">\n        <a href="#cite_note-23">\n         [23]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="16_March_(Flight_day_2)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="16_March_.28Flight_day_2.29">\n        16 March (Flight day 2)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-119&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: 16 March (Flight day 2)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Following the crew\'s wakeup call, the members of STS-119 set to work on the day\'s task of inspecting\n       <i>\n        Discovery\'s\n       </i>\n       <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_thermal_protection_system" title="Space Shuttle thermal protection system">\n        thermal protection system\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SR3_24-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SR3-24">\n         [24]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-day2nsf_25-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-day2nsf-25">\n         [25]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Using the shuttle\'s\n       <a href="/wiki/Canadarm" title="Canadarm">\n        robotic arm\n       </a>\n       and the\n       <a href="/wiki/Orbiter_Boom_Sensor_System" title="Orbiter Boom Sensor System">\n        Orbiter Boom Sensor System\n       </a>\n       (OBSS), the crew performed the five-hour inspection, and the images and video from the survey would be reviewed by the image analysis team on the ground.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SR3_24-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SR3-24">\n         [24]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In preparation for docking with the space station on flight day three, the crew performed a checkout of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Extravehicular_Mobility_Unit" title="Extravehicular Mobility Unit">\n        spacesuits\n       </a>\n       that would be used during the mission, as well as extending the ring of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Androgynous_Peripheral_Attach_System" title="Androgynous Peripheral Attach System">\n        orbital docking system\n       </a>\n       , and installing the docking system\'s centerline camera.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SR3_24-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SR3-24">\n         [24]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Initial review of the flight ascent imagery indicated no major problems with foam loss or debris strikes to the orbiter. During the day\'s Mission Management Team briefing, chairman\n       <a href="/wiki/LeRoy_E._Cain" title="LeRoy E. Cain">\n        LeRoy Cain\n       </a>\n       noted that the launch was "picture perfect" and the orbiter was in excellent condition.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-sfn2_26-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-sfn2-26">\n         [26]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Cain also noted that after an initial review of the telemetry from the launch, the hydrogen flow control valves performed as expected, with no issues seen.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-sfn2_26-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-sfn2-26">\n         [26]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="17_March_(Flight_day_3)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="17_March_.28Flight_day_3.29">\n        17 March (Flight day 3)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-119&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: 17 March (Flight day 3)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       The crew of\n       <i>\n        Discovery\n       </i>\n       got to work in the morning preparing for rendezvous and docking with the space station.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SR5_27-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SR5-27">\n         [27]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-bbc1_28-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-bbc1-28">\n         [28]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-sfnday3_29-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-sfnday3-29">\n         [29]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       After performing the\n       <a href="/wiki/Rendezvous_pitch_maneuver" title="Rendezvous pitch maneuver">\n        rendezvous pitch maneuver\n       </a>\n       (RPM) to allow the Expedition 18 crew to photograph the underside of the orbiter,\n       <i>\n        Discovery\n       </i>\n       successfully docked with the station at 21:20 UTC.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SR5_27-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SR5-27">\n         [27]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Following hatch leak checks, the hatches were opened at 23:09 UTC.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SR5_27-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SR5-27">\n         [27]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       After greeting each other, the crews had a mandatory station safety briefing, and then set to work with initial transfers, including the exchange of Magnus\'\n       <i>\n        Soyuz\n       </i>\n       seat liner for Wakata\'s. The swap of the seat liners marked Wakata officially joining the Expedition 18 crew as Flight Engineer, and Magnus became a Mission Specialist for STS-119.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SR5_27-3">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SR5-27">\n         [27]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-bbc1_28-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-bbc1-28">\n         [28]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-sfnday3_29-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-sfnday3-29">\n         [29]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       During the Mission Status briefing, Lead Flight Director Paul Dye commended Archambault on a picture perfect docking.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-sfnday3_29-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-sfnday3-29">\n         [29]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Dye said that no major issues or anomalies were being tracked, but noted that the image analysis team was still working on ascent imagery, and would be reviewing the RPM imagery before making a decision as to whether\n       <i>\n        Discovery\n       </i>\n       would require a focused inspection.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-sfnday3_29-3">\n        <a href="#cite_note-sfnday3-29">\n         [29]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="18_March_(Flight_day_4)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="18_March_.28Flight_day_4.29">\n        18 March (Flight day 4)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-119&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: 18 March (Flight day 4)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-119_S6_Handover.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1985" data-file-width="3000" height="146" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e5/STS-119_S6_Handover.jpg/220px-STS-119_S6_Handover.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e5/STS-119_S6_Handover.jpg/330px-STS-119_S6_Handover.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e5/STS-119_S6_Handover.jpg/440px-STS-119_S6_Handover.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:STS-119_S6_Handover.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         The handover of the\n         <a href="/wiki/Integrated_Truss_Structure#P5.2C_S5_trusses" title="Integrated Truss Structure">\n          S6 truss\n         </a>\n         truss segment.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-119_EVA1_Arnold01.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2847" data-file-width="4288" height="146" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/62/STS-119_EVA1_Arnold01.jpg/220px-STS-119_EVA1_Arnold01.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/62/STS-119_EVA1_Arnold01.jpg/330px-STS-119_EVA1_Arnold01.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/62/STS-119_EVA1_Arnold01.jpg/440px-STS-119_EVA1_Arnold01.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:STS-119_EVA1_Arnold01.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Mission Specialist\n         <a href="/wiki/Richard_R._Arnold" title="Richard R. Arnold">\n          Arnold\n         </a>\n         during his first spacewalk.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Following the crew\'s post-sleep activities, the two crews set to work preparing for the next day\'s spacewalk, by moving the S6 truss out of\n       <i>\n        Discovery\'s\n       </i>\n       payload bay. Due to clearance restrictions, the station\'s\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Canadarm2" title="Canadarm2">\n        robotic arm\n       </a>\n       was not able to perform the move by itself, so a series of \'handoffs\' were performed to prepare the truss for installation.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-sfn319_30-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-sfn319-30">\n         [30]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Phillips and Magnus controlled the station\'s arm, grappled the truss and moved it into a position where the shuttle\'s\n       <a href="/wiki/Canadarm" title="Canadarm">\n        robotic arm\n       </a>\n       , operated by Antonelli, could take possession.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-sfn319_30-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-sfn319-30">\n         [30]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The station arm was then moved along the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Canadarm2#Mobile_Base_System" title="Canadarm2">\n        mobile base\n       </a>\n       to a work site on the far right side, closer to the installation point. The shuttle\'s robotic arm then handed the truss back to the station\'s arm, where it remained overnight.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-sfn319_30-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-sfn319-30">\n         [30]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SR7_31-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SR7-31">\n         [31]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The crews took part in a media event with Channel One News, and performed a review of the procedures for the first EVA. Mission Specialists Swanson and Arnold spent the night in the\n       <a href="/wiki/Quest_Joint_Airlock" title="Quest Joint Airlock">\n        <i>\n         Quest\n        </i>\n        airlock\n       </a>\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Airlock_campout" title="Airlock campout">\n        camping out\n       </a>\n       in a reduced-nitrogen atmosphere, a standard procedure designed for spacewalkers to prevent decompression symptoms.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SR7_31-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SR7-31">\n         [31]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-sfn319a_32-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-sfn319a-32">\n         [32]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       During the Mission Management Team briefing, Lead ISS Flight Director\n       <a href="/wiki/Kwatsi_Alibaruho" title="Kwatsi Alibaruho">\n        Kwatsi Alibaruho\n       </a>\n       noted that the imagery specialists with the Damage Assessment Team had completed the initial review of the launch and flight day 2 photography, and a focused inspection of the orbiter would not be required.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-sfn319_30-3">\n        <a href="#cite_note-sfn319-30">\n         [30]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SR7_31-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SR7-31">\n         [31]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="19_March_(Flight_day_5,_Spacewalk_1)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="19_March_.28Flight_day_5.2C_Spacewalk_1.29">\n        19 March (Flight day 5, Spacewalk 1)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-119&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: 19 March (Flight day 5, Spacewalk 1)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       The two crews set to work following their wake up call, preparing for the first spacewalk of the mission. Swanson and Arnold exited the\n       <i>\n        Quest\n       </i>\n       airlock at 16:22 UTC to begin the installation of the S6 truss segment.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-autogenerated2_33-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-autogenerated2-33">\n         [33]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SR9_34-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SR9-34">\n         [34]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Once Swanson and Arnold were in position, Phillips and Wakata remotely controlled the station\'s robotic arm, maneuvering the truss into its final position. Swanson and Arnold then bolted the truss into place, and connected power and data cables, which allowed the ground team to begin remote activation of the segment.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SR9_34-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SR9-34">\n         [34]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The two spacewalkers also removed launch locks, stowed a keel pin, removed and jettisoned four thermal covers, and deployed the blanket boxes that hold the solar arrays in place during launch.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-sfn319_30-4">\n        <a href="#cite_note-sfn319-30">\n         [30]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-sfn319b_35-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-sfn319b-35">\n         [35]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The spacewalk ended at 21:11 UTC, for a total time of 6 hours, 7 minutes.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-sfn319_30-5">\n        <a href="#cite_note-sfn319-30">\n         [30]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Initially scheduled for flight day 8, managers on the ground decided to move up the deployment of the solar arrays, following the decision that a focused inspection would not be required. It was decided that the deployment of the arrays would be performed on flight day 6, prior to the mission\'s second spacewalk, in case any issues arose that required a spacewalk to resolve.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SR9_34-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SR9-34">\n         [34]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="20_March_(Flight_day_6)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="20_March_.28Flight_day_6.29">\n        20 March (Flight day 6)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-119&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: 20 March (Flight day 6)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Joseph_Acaba_using_ergometer.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2848" data-file-width="4288" height="146" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/29/Joseph_Acaba_using_ergometer.jpg/220px-Joseph_Acaba_using_ergometer.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/29/Joseph_Acaba_using_ergometer.jpg/330px-Joseph_Acaba_using_ergometer.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/29/Joseph_Acaba_using_ergometer.jpg/440px-Joseph_Acaba_using_ergometer.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Joseph_Acaba_using_ergometer.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         On flight day six, Mission Specialist\n         <a href="/wiki/Joseph_M._Acaba" title="Joseph M. Acaba">\n          Acaba\n         </a>\n         used the shuttle\'s ergometer before the crews began deploying the solar arrays.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-119_EVA_3_Joseph_Acaba.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2032" data-file-width="3072" height="146" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cd/STS-119_EVA_3_Joseph_Acaba.jpg/220px-STS-119_EVA_3_Joseph_Acaba.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cd/STS-119_EVA_3_Joseph_Acaba.jpg/330px-STS-119_EVA_3_Joseph_Acaba.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cd/STS-119_EVA_3_Joseph_Acaba.jpg/440px-STS-119_EVA_3_Joseph_Acaba.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:STS-119_EVA_3_Joseph_Acaba.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         The S6 truss solar array unfurled.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       As part of the re-planning for the mission, the crews set to work in the morning deploying the solar wings on the S6 truss.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-sfn320_36-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-sfn320-36">\n         [36]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SR11_37-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SR11-37">\n         [37]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       To prepare for the extension of the arrays, the station was maneuvered into a position that allowed constant sunlight to hit the arrays, which allowed them to warm up and prevent what the mission team calls \'stiction\', or a sticky friction that happens after the arrays have been in storage for an extended period of time.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SR11_37-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SR11-37">\n         [37]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The unfurling of the arrays started at 15:06 UTC, beginning with the channel 1B array. Commanding the unit from the station, Philips paused at the halfway point, and allowed the array to rest in the sun for approximately 45 minutes, and then completed the extension.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-sfn320b_38-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-sfn320b-38">\n         [38]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       After successfully extending the 1B array, the astronauts started the 3B array extension at 16:35 UTC. The 3B array was expected to be more difficult to extend, as it had been packed in the blanket box for eight years.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-sfn320_36-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-sfn320-36">\n         [36]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       As with the first, a pause at halfway was performed to allow the arrays to heat up in the sun. While some stiction was seen, once the final extension began all the slats flattened out, and the arrays were fully deployed at 17:17 UTC.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-sfn320b_38-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-sfn320b-38">\n         [38]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The addition of the final set of solar panels brings the station\'s power output to 120\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kilowatt" title="Kilowatt">\n        kilowatts\n       </a>\n       , and doubles the scientific power to 30 kilowatts.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SR11_37-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SR11-37">\n         [37]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The station\'s surface area of the arrays is just under one acre, or 38,400 square feet.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SR11_37-3">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SR11-37">\n         [37]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Later in the day, Fincke, Lonchakov, Wakata and Magnus participated in a media event with\n       <a href="/wiki/Reuters" title="Reuters">\n        Reuters\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Voice_of_America" title="Voice of America">\n        Voice of America\n       </a>\n       , and the\n       <a href="/wiki/Pittsburgh_Post-Gazette" title="Pittsburgh Post-Gazette">\n        Pittsburgh Post-Gazette\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SR10_39-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SR10-39">\n         [39]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       During the Mission Status briefing, Alibaruho expressed how pleased the teams on the ground were with the successful deployment of the arrays, and commended the crew on the deployment activities.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-sfn320_36-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-sfn320-36">\n         [36]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Mission Management Team Chairman LeRoy Cain noted that the team was working on a revised timetable to allow critical experiment samples to return to earth safely. The samples need to be kept in a cold environment, and in the event weather delayed the landing, the team evaluated the best way to preserve the samples. The team approved a revised flight plan that allows\n       <i>\n        Discovery\n       </i>\n       to delay hatch closure and undocking slightly, to allow the samples to be kept inside the station\'s freezer longer, while still protecting the landing date of 28 March.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-sfn320_36-3">\n        <a href="#cite_note-sfn320-36">\n         [36]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Instead of closing the hatch the night before undocking, the hatch would be closed on the same day, flight day eleven.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-sfn320_36-4">\n        <a href="#cite_note-sfn320-36">\n         [36]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <table class="cquote" role="presentation" style="margin:auto; border-collapse: collapse; border: none; background-color: transparent; width: auto;">\n       <tr>\n        <td style="width: 20px; vertical-align: top; border: none; color: #B2B7F2; font-size: 40px; font-family: \'Times New Roman\', Times, serif; font-weight: bold; line-height: .6em; text-align: left; padding: 10px 10px;">\n         \xe2\x80\x9c\n        </td>\n        <td style="vertical-align: top; border: none; padding: 4px 10px;">\n         "It was a truly fantastic day in space. The International Space Station team and its partnerships are on cloud nine with the completion of the integrated truss assembly, as well as the finalization of our electrical power grid on the space station. It took years to get here. We had some struggles along the way, but it\'s a major accomplishment for NASA and the partnership team."\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-sfn320_36-5">\n          <a href="#cite_note-sfn320-36">\n           [36]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n         \xe2\x80\x93 Dan Hartman, Space Station Mission Management Team Chairman\n        </td>\n        <td style="width: 20px; vertical-align: bottom; border: none; color: #B2B7F2; font-size: 40px; font-family: \'Times New Roman\', Times, serif; font-weight: bold; line-height: .6em; text-align: right; padding: 10px 10px;">\n         \xe2\x80\x9d\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="21_March_(Flight_day_7,_Spacewalk_2)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="21_March_.28Flight_day_7.2C_Spacewalk_2.29">\n        21 March (Flight day 7, Spacewalk 2)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-119&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: 21 March (Flight day 7, Spacewalk 2)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:UCCAS.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="350" data-file-width="412" height="187" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6f/UCCAS.jpg/220px-UCCAS.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6f/UCCAS.jpg/330px-UCCAS.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/6/6f/UCCAS.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:UCCAS.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         The unpressurized cargo carrier attachment system (UCCAS)\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:ISS_March_2009.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1856" data-file-width="2464" height="166" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/ISS_March_2009.jpg/220px-ISS_March_2009.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/ISS_March_2009.jpg/330px-ISS_March_2009.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/ISS_March_2009.jpg/440px-ISS_March_2009.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:ISS_March_2009.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         ISS after departure of STS-119\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Swanson and Acaba began the second spacewalk at 16:51 UTC. They loosened bolts, installed foot restraints and prepared tools so that the\n       <a href="/wiki/STS-127" title="STS-127">\n        STS-127\n       </a>\n       spacewalkers could more easily change out the Port 6 truss batteries later this year. On the Japanese\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Japanese_Experiment_Module" title="Japanese Experiment Module">\n        <i>\n         Kibo\n        </i>\n        laboratory\n       </a>\n       they installed a second\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Global_Positioning_Satellite" title="Global Positioning Satellite">\n        Global Positioning Satellite\n       </a>\n       antenna. They photographed areas of radiator panels extended from the Port 1 and Starboard 1 trusses and reconfigured connectors at a patch panel on the Zenith 1 truss that power Control Moment\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Gyroscopes" title="Gyroscopes">\n        Gyroscopes\n       </a>\n       . After struggling with a pin that kept an\n       <i>\n        Unpressurized Cargo Carrier Attachment System\n       </i>\n       (UCCAS) from fully deploying, they tied UCCAS safely in place. The spacewalk ended at 23:21 UTC, for a time of six hours and thirty minutes.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-sfn321d_40-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-sfn321d-40">\n         [40]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="22_March_(Flight_day_8)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="22_March_.28Flight_day_8.29">\n        22 March (Flight day 8)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-119&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: 22 March (Flight day 8)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       At 20:31 UTC,\n       <i>\n        Discovery\n       </i>\n       rotated the shuttle-station complex 180 degrees, to avoid a piece of orbital debris. At 23:23,\n       <i>\n        Discovery\n       </i>\n       began rotating the station back to normal attitude, with the shuttle in \'back\'.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Fincke continued to work on the Urine Processor Assembly, while Acaba and Arnold entered the\n       <i>\n        Quest\n       </i>\n       Airlock to prepare for the mission\'s third spacewalk.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-41">\n        <a href="#cite_note-41">\n         [41]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="23_March_(Flight_day_9,_Spacewalk_3)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="23_March_.28Flight_day_9.2C_Spacewalk_3.29">\n        23 March (Flight day 9, Spacewalk 3)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-119&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: 23 March (Flight day 9, Spacewalk 3)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Acaba and Arnold completed the mission\'s third spacewalk. They helped robotic arm operators relocate the Crew Equipment Translation Aid (CETA) cart from the Port 1 to Starboard 1 truss segment, installed a new coupler on the CETA cart, and lubricated snares on the space station\'s robotic arm.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       They were unable to deploy the Port 3 unpressurized cargo carrier attachment system (UCCAS). They secured the UCCAS in place until engineers can evaluate the problem. Mission Control cancelled the installation of a similar payload attachment system on the starboard side. The port UCCAS was deployed successfully during\n       <a href="/wiki/STS-127" title="STS-127">\n        STS-127\n       </a>\n       by releasing the stuck pin with a custom made tool.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The spacewalk lasted six hours, 27 minutes. It began at 15:37 UTC and concluded at 22:04 UTC.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-42">\n        <a href="#cite_note-42">\n         [42]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="24_March_(Flight_day_10)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="24_March_.28Flight_day_10.29">\n        24 March (Flight day 10)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-119&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: 24 March (Flight day 10)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Barack_Obama_calls_ISS.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3413" data-file-width="5120" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/28/Barack_Obama_calls_ISS.jpg/220px-Barack_Obama_calls_ISS.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/28/Barack_Obama_calls_ISS.jpg/330px-Barack_Obama_calls_ISS.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/28/Barack_Obama_calls_ISS.jpg/440px-Barack_Obama_calls_ISS.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Barack_Obama_calls_ISS.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_United_States" title="President of the United States">\n          President\n         </a>\n         <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">\n          Obama\n         </a>\n         , members of\n         <a href="/wiki/United_States_Congress" title="United States Congress">\n          Congress\n         </a>\n         , and schoolchildren speak with astronauts aboard the ISS.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       At 17:05 UTC, all crew members aboard\n       <i>\n        Discovery\n       </i>\n       and the space station gathered in the station\'s\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Harmony_module" title="Harmony module">\n        <i>\n         Harmony\n        </i>\n        module\n       </a>\n       and spoke to the President of the United States, members of the\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States_Congress" title="United States Congress">\n        United States Congress\n       </a>\n       , and students during a joint news conference.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-43">\n        <a href="#cite_note-43">\n         [43]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="25_March_(Flight_day_11)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="25_March_.28Flight_day_11.29">\n        25 March (Flight day 11)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-119&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: 25 March (Flight day 11)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Crew members from space shuttle\n       <i>\n        Discovery\n       </i>\n       and the International Space Station closed their respective hatches at 17:59 UTC. The space shuttle undocked from the International Space Station at 19:53 UTC.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-44">\n        <a href="#cite_note-44">\n         [44]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="26_March_(Flight_day_12)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="26_March_.28Flight_day_12.29">\n        26 March (Flight day 12)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-119&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: 26 March (Flight day 12)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-119_Discovery_landing01.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2008" data-file-width="3000" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/44/STS-119_Discovery_landing01.jpg/220px-STS-119_Discovery_landing01.jpg" <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:STS-119_Discovery_landing01.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Space Shuttle\n         <i>\n          Discovery\n         </i>\n         lands after completing its STS-119 mission.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-119_crew_after_landing.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2008" data-file-width="3000" height="147" <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:STS-119_crew_after_landing.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Members of the STS-119 crew pose after landing. L-R: Commander Lee Archambault, Pilot Tony Antonelli and Mission Specialists Joseph Acaba, Steve Swanson, Richard Arnold and John Phillips.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Antonelli used the shuttle\'s robotic arm to grapple the Orbiter Boom Sensor System enabling the cameras and laser sensors to scan\n       <i>\n        Discovery\n       </i>\n       for signs of damage from orbital debris.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-45">\n        <a href="#cite_note-45">\n         [45]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="27_March_(Flight_day_13)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="27_March_.28Flight_day_13.29">\n        27 March (Flight day 13)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-119&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: 27 March (Flight day 13)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       The crew stowed items in the crew cabin and completed a check out the orbiter\'s flight control surfaces.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-46">\n        <a href="#cite_note-46">\n         [46]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="28_March_(Flight_day_14,_Landing)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="28_March_.28Flight_day_14.2C_Landing.29">\n        28 March (Flight day 14, Landing)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-119&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: 28 March (Flight day 14, Landing)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Following the wake up call, the crew on board\n       <i>\n        Discovery\n       </i>\n       got to work preparing for entry. After the first landing opportunity was waved off due to high wind concerns, the team on the ground gave the crew a \'go\' to proceed with the second opportunity.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-home_1-4">\n        <a href="#cite_note-home-1">\n         [1]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Following the deorbit burn, the orbiter landed successfully at 15:13 EDT.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-home_1-5">\n        <a href="#cite_note-home-1">\n         [1]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Extra-vehicular_activity">\n        Extra-vehicular activity\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-119&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Extra-vehicular activity">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <p>\n       Three\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Extra-vehicular_activity" title="Extra-vehicular activity">\n        spacewalks\n       </a>\n       were scheduled and completed during STS-119. The cumulative time in extra-vehicular activity during the mission was 19 hours and 4 minutes.\n      </p>\n      <table class="wikitable">\n       <tr>\n        <th style="width: 5em;">\n         EVA\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         Spacewalkers\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         Start (\n         <a href="/wiki/Coordinated_Universal_Time" title="Coordinated Universal Time">\n          UTC\n         </a>\n         )\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         End (UTC)\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         Duration\n        </th>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td rowspan="2">\n         EVA 1\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/Steven_Swanson" title="Steven Swanson">\n          Steven R. class="mw-headline" id="Wake-up_calls">\n        Wake-up calls\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-119&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Wake-up calls">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <p>\n       A tradition for NASA human spaceflights since the days of\n       <a href="/wiki/Project_Gemini" title="Project Gemini">\n        Gemini\n       </a>\n       , is that mission crews are played a special musical track at the start of each day in space. Each track is specially chosen, often by their family, and usually has a special meaning to an individual member of the crew, or is applicable to their daily activities.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-53">\n        <a href="#cite_note-53">\n         [53]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-wakeup_54-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-wakeup-54">\n         [54]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        <b>\n         Day 2\n        </b>\n        : "\n        <a href="/wiki/Free_Bird" title="Free Bird">\n         Free Bird\n        </a>\n        " performed by\n        <a href="/wiki/Lynyrd_Skynyrd" title="Lynyrd Skynyrd">\n         Lynyrd Skynyrd\n        </a>\n        , played for Pilot\n        <a href="/wiki/Dominic_A._Antonelli" title="Dominic A. Antonelli">\n         Tony Antonelli\n        </a>\n        .\n        <a class="external text" href="http://spaceflight.nasa.gov/gallery/audio/shuttle/sts-119/wave/fd2.wav" rel="nofollow">\n
